### <a id="inductive-types-h-s-p-and-v">Inductive Types H, S, P, and V</a>

This section presents the [UALib.Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="1654" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1658" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="1666" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="1678" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="1692" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="1699" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphism closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2378" class="Comment">--Closure wrt H</a>

  <a id="H.hiso"></a><a id="2695" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#2695" class="InductiveConstructor">hiso</a>  <a id="2701" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2703" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2704" <!-- We say that a class 𝒦 is **closed under** `H` (or `H`-**closed**) provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

--------------------------------

#### <a id="subalgebra-closure">Subalgebra closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras that are closed under the taking of subalgebras as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3143" class="Comment">--Closure wrt S</a>
<a id="3159" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="3164" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3166" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3167" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3167" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3169" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3171" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3173" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="3181" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="3183" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3183" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3185" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3187" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3192" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3193" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3201" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3167" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3203" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3204" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3206" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3207" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3210" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3167" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3211" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3214" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="3217" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3222" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3223" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3231" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3232" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3167" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3234" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3236" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3237" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3239" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3240" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3242" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3243" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a><a id="3245" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3246" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3167" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3248" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3250" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3251" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3254" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="S.sbase"></a><a id="3262" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3262" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="3268" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3270" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3271" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3271" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3273" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3275" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3283" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3167" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3285" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3286" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3288" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3290" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3271" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3292" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3294" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3183" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3296" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3298" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3971" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="3307" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3271" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3169" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="3311" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3313" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3315" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3183" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3183" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `S` (or `S`-**closed**) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` -->

-----------------------------------------

#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing classes of algebras closed under arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3945" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3950" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3950" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3952" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3953" <a id="3973" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="3978" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3979" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3987" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3989" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3990" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="3992" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="3995" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3996" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3999" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4001" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="4006" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4007" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4015" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4016" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4018" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4020" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3955" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4021" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4023" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" id="4318" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#676" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="4320" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4267" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="4322" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719"   <a id="P.prodw"></a><a id="4330" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4330" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a>  <a id="4337" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4339" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4340" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4366" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4368" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4369" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4371" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4373" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="4376" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4376" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="4378" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4381" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="4383" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4376" class="Bound">i</a><a id="4384" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4394" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4396" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3969" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="4397" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4399" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4401" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#676" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="4403" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4350" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="4405" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719"   <a id="P.pisou"></a><a id="4413" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4413" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a>  <a id="4420" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4422" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4423" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4479" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4481" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4483" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4440"   <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4493" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4493" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4500" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4502" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4503" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4505" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4505" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4507" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4509" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4517" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4519" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4520" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4522" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4524" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4526" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4528" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3950" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4529" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4530" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3953" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4531" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4533" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3955" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4534" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4536" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3969" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4538" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4540" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4503" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4542" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4544" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4505" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4546" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4548" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4505" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4550" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4552" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3950" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4554" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3969" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

<!-- A class 𝒦 is **closed under** `P` (or `P`-**closed**) provided `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. -->

-----------------------------------------------

#### <a id="variety-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will typically denote it by `V`.

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="5220" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="5225" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5225" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5227" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5228" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5230" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5230" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5232" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5234" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="5242" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5244" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5246" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5248" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5253" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5254" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5262" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5264" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5265" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5267" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5270" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5271" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5274" class="Symbol">:</a>
 <a id="5277" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5282" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5283" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5291" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5292" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5294" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5296" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5230" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5297" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5300" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5302" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a><a id="5304" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5305" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5307" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5230" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5310" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5313" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="V.vbase"></a><a id="5321" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5321" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a>  <a id="5328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5330" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5331" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5331" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5335" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5343" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5345" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5346" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5348" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5350" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5331" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5352" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5354" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5356" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5358" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3971" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="5367" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5331" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5369" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5230" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="5371" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5373" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5225" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5375" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="V.vssubw"></a><a id="5676" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5676" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="5683" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5685" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5686" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5686" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5688" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5688" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5690" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5692" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5700" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5702" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5703" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5705" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5707" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5686" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5709" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5711" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5225" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5712" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5713" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5228" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5714" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5716" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5230" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5717" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5719" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5721" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5723" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5688" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5725" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1804" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="5727" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5686" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5729" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5731" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5688" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5733" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5735" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5225" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we formally represent what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="6212" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6212" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="6223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6225" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6226" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6226" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6228" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6230" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6238" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="6240" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6240" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6242" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6244" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6249" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6250" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6258" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6226" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6260" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6261" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6263" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6266" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6226" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6267" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6270" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6272" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6275" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6226" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6277" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="6279" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6212" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="6289" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6290" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6290" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6291" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6293" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6293" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6295" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6297" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#5225" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6298" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6299" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6290" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6300" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6302" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6290" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6303" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6305" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6293" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="6307" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3001" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6309" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6293" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="6312" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6312" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="6320" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6322" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6323" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6323" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6325" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6327" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6335" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6337" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6339" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6340" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6343" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6323" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6344" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="6345" href="universes.html#527" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="6347" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>

-------------------------------

#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties since we will need them later.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6677" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s expansive.</a>
<a id="P-expa"></a><a id="6736" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6736" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="6743" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6745" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6746" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6746" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6748" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6750" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="6758" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6760" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6762" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6764" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6769" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6770" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6778" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6746" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6780" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6781" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6783" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6786" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6746" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6787" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6790" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6792" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6794" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#3001" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="6796" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3950" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="6797" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6798" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6746" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6799" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6801" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6746" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6802" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6804" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6760" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
<a id="6806" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6736" class="Function">P-expa</a><a id="6812" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6813" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6813" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6814" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6816" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6816" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="6817" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6819" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6820" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6820" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6821" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6823" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6823" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="6826" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6828" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4413" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="6833" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6834" class="Argument">𝑨</a> <a id="6836" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6838" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6839" href="UALib.Algebras.Lifts.html#3971" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6848" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6820" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6850" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6813" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6851" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="6854" class="Argument">𝑩</a> <a id="6856" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6858" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6820" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6859" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6861" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6862" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4045" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="6868" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#6823" class="Bound">KA</a><a id="6870" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6872" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6873" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2465" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="6879" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4457" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="6889" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6892" class="Comment">-- P is a closure operator; in particular, it&#39;s idempotent.</a>

<a id="7730" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7510" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7737" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7737" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7742" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7743" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3384" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="7747" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7748" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7748" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7749" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7751" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7751" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7752" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7754" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7754" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7757" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7757" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7760" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7762" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7764" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3384" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="7769" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7770" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7510" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7777" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7737" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7782" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7754" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="7784" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7786" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7757" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="7790" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7510" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7797" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7797" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7802" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7803" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3463" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="7808" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7809" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7809" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7810" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7812" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7812" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7813" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7815" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7815" class="Bound">sA</a> <a id="7818" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7818" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="7821" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7823" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7825" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3463" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="7831" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7832" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7510" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7839" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7797" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7844" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7815" class="Bound">sA</a><a id="7846" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7848" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7818" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="7852" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7510" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7859" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7859" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7864" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7865" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3527" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7870" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7870" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7872" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7872" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7874" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7876" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7878" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3527" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="7883" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7884" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7510" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="7891" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7859" class="Bound">ante</a> <a id="7896" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7870" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7897" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7899" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#7872" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="subalgebra→S"></a><a id="8111" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8111" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="8124" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8126" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8127" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8127" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8129" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8129" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8131" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8133" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="8141" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8143" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8143" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8145" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8147" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="8152" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8153" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8161" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8127" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8163" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8164" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8166" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8169" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8127" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8170" class="Symbol">)}</a>
               <a id="8188" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8189" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8189" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8191" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8193" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8201" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8202" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8127" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8204" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="8206" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8129" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="8207" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8209" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8210" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8212" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8214" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8189" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="8216" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1997" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="8236" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8143" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

   <a id="9937" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9937" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="9940" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9942" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1538" class="Function">Subalgebra</a> <a id="9953" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9955" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9881" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9958" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="9963" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9937" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="9966" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9968" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10375" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="9972" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="9974" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9881" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="9977" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a>
   <a id="9982" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9982" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="9987" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9989" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9855" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9991" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="9993" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="9995" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9937" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="9998" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>
   <a id="10003" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9982" class="Function">A≅SA</a> <a id="10008" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10010" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10014" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10016" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10020" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9881" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10023" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a>
   <a id="10028" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10028" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="10030" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10032" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9846" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10034" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1997" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10054" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#8602" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
   <a id="10059" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10028" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="10061" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10063" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10065" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9881" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10068" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10070" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10072" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9937" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="10075" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a>  <a id="10078" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10080" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10456" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="10084" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10086" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9881" class="Function">AS</a> <a id="10089" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10452" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="10091" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10093" href="MGS-MLTT.html#2929" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10095" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10096" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3686" class="Function">TRANS-≅</a> <a id="10104" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10105" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2465" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="10111" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9861" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="10114" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10116" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#9982" class="Function">A≅SA</a><a id="10120" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="10486" class="Symbol">→</a>                <a id="10503" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10467" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10505" href="UALib.Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#1997" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10526" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3950" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="10527" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10528" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10421" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10529" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10531" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10421" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10532" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10534" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#10437" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10535" class="Symbol">)</a>

The next lemma would be too obvoius to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S⊆SP"></a><a id="11173" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11173" class="Function">S⊆SP</a> <a id="11178" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11180" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="11181" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11181" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="11183" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11183" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="11185" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11187" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="11195" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="11197" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11197" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="11199" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11201" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="11206" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11207" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="11215" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11181" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="11217" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="11218" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="11220" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="11223" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#11181" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="11224" class="Symbol">)}</a>

  <a id="12922" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12922" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="12927" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12929" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12612" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12932" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#861" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="12934" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#12552" class="Bound">𝑩</a>

</pre>

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the short term objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

  <a id="14311" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14294" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="14313" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14315" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6367" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="14318" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1901" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="14322" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#13638" class="Function">B≅SA</a>

</pre>

#### PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="14516" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="14523" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14523" class="Module">_</a> <a id="14525" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14526" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14526" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14530" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="14538" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="14540" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14540" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14542" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14544" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="14549" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14550" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="14558" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14526" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="14560" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="14561" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14563" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14566" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14526" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14567" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14570" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14571" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14571" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="14575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14577" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="14585" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14586" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14589" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14526" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14590" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14592" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14595" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14526" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="14596" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="14599" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="14607" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14607" class="Function">ov𝓾</a> <a id="14611" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14613" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a>
 <a id="14623" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14607" class="Function">ov𝓾</a> <a id="14627" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14629" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="14632" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#14526" class="Bound">𝓤</a>

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this module with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play in our formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem.

</pre>


#### <a id="products-of-classes">Products of classes</a>

Next we formally state and prove that, given an arbitrary class 𝒦 of algebras, the product of all algebras in the class S(𝒦) belongs to SP(𝒦). That is, ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦 ). This turns out to be a nontrivial exercise. In fact, it is not immediately obvious (at least not to this author) how one expresses the product of an entire class of algebras as a dependent type. Nonetheless, after a number of failed attempts, the right type revealed itself. (Not surprisingly, now that we have it, it seems almost obvious.)

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="17835" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product"></a><a id="17842" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17842" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="17856" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17857" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17857" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17859" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17861" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="17869" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17871" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17871" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17873" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17875" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17880" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17881" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17889" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17857" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17891" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17892" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17894" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17897" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17857" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17898" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17901" class="Keyword">where</a>

</pre>

First, we define the type that will serve to index the class (as well as the product of its members), as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.ℑ"></a><a id="18050" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18052" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18054" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18055" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18055" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18057" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18059" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18067" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18069" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="18072" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18077" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18078" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18086" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18055" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18088" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18089" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18091" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18094" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18055" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18095" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18097" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18099" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18100" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18103" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18055" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18104" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18106" href="universes.html#758" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
 <a id="18109" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18111" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18112" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18112" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18113" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18115" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18115" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18117" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18119" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18121" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18121" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18123" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18125" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18126" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18134" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18112" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18136" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18137" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18139" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18141" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18121" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18143" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18145" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18115" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Taking the product over this index type ℑ requires a function like the following, which takes an index (i : ℑ) and returns the corresponding algebra.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.𝔄"></a><a id="18326" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18326" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="18328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18330" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18331" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18331" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18333" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18335" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18343" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18345" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18345" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18347" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18349" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18354" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18355" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18363" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18331" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18365" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18366" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18368" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18371" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18331" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18372" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="18375" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18377" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18379" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18345" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18381" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18383" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18391" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18331" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18393" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18396" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18326" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18397" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18398" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18398" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18399" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18401" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18401" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18402" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18404" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18406" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18409" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18409" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18411" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18413" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18414" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="18416" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18401" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18417" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18420" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18422" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18424" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18409" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18426" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Finally, the product of all members of 𝒦 is represented as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.class-product"></a><a id="18525" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18525" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18539" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18541" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18542" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18542" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18544" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18546" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18554" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18556" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18558" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18563" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18564" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18572" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18542" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18574" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18575" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18577" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18580" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18542" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18581" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18583" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18585" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18594" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18597" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18542" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18598" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18600" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18603" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18525" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="18617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18618" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18618" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18619" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18621" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18621" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18623" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18625" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#676" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18627" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18629" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18326" class="Function">𝔄</a><a id="18630" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18631" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18618" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18632" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18634" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18621" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18635" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18637" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Alternatively, we could have defined the class product in a way that explicitly displays the index, like so.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-product.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="18777" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18777" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="18792" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18794" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18795" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18795" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18797" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18799" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="18807" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18809" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18811" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="18816" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18817" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18825" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18795" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18827" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18828" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="18830" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18833" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18795" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18834" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18836" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18838" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18846" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18847" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18850" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18795" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18851" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18853" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="18856" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18777" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a><a id="18870" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18871" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18871" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18872" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18874" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18874" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="18876" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18878" href="UALib.Algebras.Products.html#676" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="18880" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="18882" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18883" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18883" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18885" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18888" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="18890" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18890" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18892" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="18894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18895" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="18903" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18871" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18905" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="18906" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18908" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="18910" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18890" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18912" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="18914" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18874" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18915" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18918" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18920" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="18922" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18883" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="18924" href="UALib.Prelude.Preliminaries.html#10371" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

If `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, then we can think of the pair `(𝑨 , p) ∈ ℑ 𝒦` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p)` (which is obviously `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} )` onto the `(𝑨 , p)`-th component.


#### ⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)
Finally, we prove the result that plays a leading role in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem---namely, that our newly defined class product ⨅ ( 𝔄{𝓤}{𝒦} ) belongs to SP(𝒦).

As we just saw, the (informal) product ⨅ S(𝒦) of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as ⨅ ( 𝔄 {𝓤}{S(𝒦)} ), and our goal is to prove that this product belongs to SP(𝒦). We can do this by first proving that the product belongs to PS(𝒦) (in `class-prod-s-∈-ps`) and then applying the PS⊆SP lemma above.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="19725" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-product-inclusions"></a><a id="19732" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19732" class="Module">class-product-inclusions</a> <a id="19757" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19758" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19760" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19762" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a><a id="19770" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19772" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19773" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19773" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19775" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19777" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#1082" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19782" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19783" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19791" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19793" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19794" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19796" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19799" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19800" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19803" class="Keyword">where</a>
 <a id="19810" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="19815" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#17842" class="Module">class-product</a> <a id="19829" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19830" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19832" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19834" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19835" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19837" class="Argument">𝒦</a> <a id="19839" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19841" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19773" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19842" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.𝓸𝓿𝓾"></a><a id="19845" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a> <a id="19849" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19851" href="universes.html#551" class="Postulate">Universe</a>
 <a id="19861" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a> <a id="19865" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19867" href="UALib.Relations.Congruences.html#933" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19870" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a>

 <a id="class-product-inclusions.class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="19874" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19874" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19892" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19894" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18525" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19908" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19909" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19910" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19911" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19912" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19914" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19915" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19917" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19773" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19918" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19920" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19923" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3950" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="19924" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19925" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19928" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19930" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19933" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19935" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19936" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="19937" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19938" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19939" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19941" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19944" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19946" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19773" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19947" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="19951" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19874" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19969" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19971" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#4413" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="19976" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19977" class="Argument">𝓤</a> <a id="19979" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19982" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19985" class="Symbol">)}{</a><a id="19988" class="Argument">𝓦</a> <a id="19990" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19992" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19993" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="19996" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="19999" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20289" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="20006" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20007" href="UALib.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6367" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="20010" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1901" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="20014" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20364" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="20019" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="20023" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="20032" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20032" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="20035" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20035" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="20039" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20041" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18050" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="20043" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20044" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="20045" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20046" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20047" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20049" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19758" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="20050" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20052" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19773" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20053" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20055" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20057" href="UALib.Algebras.Algebras.html#813" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20065" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20066" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20069" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20071" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#1882" class="Bound">𝑆</a>

 <a id="20469" class="Comment">-- So, since PS⊆SP, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class 𝒦 belongs to SP(𝒦).</a>
 <a id="class-product-inclusions.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="20569" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#20569" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="20587" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20589" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a><a id="20596" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20597" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20600" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20602" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19845" class="Function">𝓸𝓿𝓾</a><a id="20605" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20607" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20609" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#18525" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="20623" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20624" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="20626" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19773" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20627" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20629" href="UALib.Relations.Unary.html#2719" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="20631" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3164" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="20632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20633" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#3950" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="20635" href="UALib.Varieties.Varieties.html#19773" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="20636" class="Symbol">)</a>
